<tr>

</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">String Quartet in B-flat major
</td></tr>
<tr>

</td></tr>

</td></tr>

</th>
<td>4 movements
<ol><li>Vivace assai (B-flat major)
</li><li>Adagio ma non troppo (E-flat major)
</li><li>Minuet - Trio (B-flat major)
</li><li>Finale. Presto (B-flat major)
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
